\put(43.2,-219.38){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Abstract—Hair has held a significant position in human }
\put(29.64,-229.7){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}society throughout history. However, with time, issues like }
\put(29.64,-240.14){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environmental pollution, social concerns, and improper use of }
\put(29.64,-250.46){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}various chemicals have exacerbated the problem of hair loss }
\put(29.64,-260.81){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}among people. This issue is now affecting individuals at a }
\put(29.64,-271.13){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}younger age, demonstrating a trend towards earlier onset. As }
\put(29.64,-281.57){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the demand for hair loss treatment has grown, various }
\put(29.64,-291.89){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}products such as hair loss shampoos and medications have }
\put(29.64,-302.21){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}emerged. Additionally, advancements in technology have }
\put(29.64,-312.53){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}made it possible for at-home medical devices to become }
\put(29.64,-322.97){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}readily available. In 2020, South Korean company LG }
\put(29.64,-333.29){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Electronics introduced its hair care product, LG Pra.L }
\put(29.64,-343.61){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Medihair, which garnered considerable attention. However, }
\put(29.64,-353.93){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it's important to note that treating hair loss is not an overnight }
\put(29.64,-364.25){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}process and requires consistent, long-term usage. To prevent }
\put(29.64,-374.69){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}individuals from giving up due to a lack of immediate results, }
\put(29.64,-385.01){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}we have incorporated features like reminders and visual }
\put(29.64,-395.33){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}comparison charts of treatment progress in our device. These }
\put(29.64,-405.65){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enhancements provide users with a more intuitive way to }
\put(29.64,-416.09){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}monitor their hair loss treatment. Furthermore, we offer }
\put(29.64,-426.41){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}personalized preventive and treatment solutions based on }
\put(29.64,-436.75){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}users' age and scalp condition. We also recommend }
\put(29.64,-447.07){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}medications and shampoos that can be used in conjunction }
\put(29.64,-457.51){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}with the Pra.L Medihair device. In essence, this application }
\put(29.64,-467.83){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}aims to assist users in a more effective utilization of the Pra.L }
\put(29.64,-478.27){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Medihair machine for hair loss treatment. }
\put(43.32,-498.55){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Keywords—visualization, personalized, effective }
\put(43.32,-514.87){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(97.22,-532.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Table I:Role Assignments }
\put(31.32,-546.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Roles  Name Task descriptions and etc. }
\end{picture}

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(280.13,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(109.1,-52.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}I. INTRODUCTION  }
\put(29.64,-69.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}A. Motivation }
\put(44.064,-84.02002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Hair is becoming a symbol of youth as the desire to }
\put(29.64,-94.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}maintain healthy youth naturally emerges as life spans }
\put(29.64,-105.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}increase and social activities increase in line with the rapid }
\put(29.64,-116.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}changes in modern society. Hair originally has the purpose }
\put(29.64,-127.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of maintaining body temperature and protecting the head, }
\put(29.64,-138.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}but over time, it has changed into one of the means of }
\put(29.64,-149.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}expressing one's personality. Throughout history, and in }
\put(29.64,-160.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}most (although not all) civilizations, scalp hair has been }
\put(29.64,-171.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}associated with positive signals such as beauty and power }
\put(29.64,-182.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}but Baldness or hair loss on the other hand has a negative }
\put(29.64,-193.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}attribute [1].  }
\put(44.064,-210.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Today, the demand for various hairstyles increases the }
\put(29.64,-221.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}frequency of physical and chemical beauty, resulting in }
\put(29.64,-231.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}damage not only to the hair but also to the scalp, causing }
\put(29.64,-242.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hair loss. As a result, interest in scalp care for healthy scalp }
\put(29.64,-253.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and beautiful hair is increasing, and various hair care }
\put(29.64,-264.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}products are being created for people who are severely }
\put(29.64,-275.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}stressed by hair loss. In terms of hair loss, not only genetic }
\put(29.64,-286.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}factors, which are fundamental reasons, but also acquired }
\put(29.64,-297.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}factors such as environmental pollution, stress due to social }
\put(29.64,-308.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}life, and hormonal secretion abnormalities caused by }
\put(29.64,-319.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}changes in negative eating habits are increasing. Hair loss, }
\put(29.64,-330.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}which used to be a symbol of aging, has become lower in }
\put(29.64,-341.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}age, with the average incidence of hair loss for men from }
\put(29.64,-352.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}34.1 in 2005 to 31.6 in 2010, and young college students in }
\put(29.64,-363.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}their 20s are also seriously considering hair loss [2].  }
\put(44.064,-380.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In addition to the increase in hair loss among young men }
\put(29.64,-391.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in their 20s and 30s, women's hair loss is also increasing due }
\put(29.64,-401.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to malnutrition, perm, dyeing, and drying caused by }
\put(29.64,-412.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}excessive diet, and the hair loss market is expanding rapidly }
\put(29.64,-423.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}due to this increase in the hair loss population, and the hair }
\put(29.64,-434.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}loss-related industry has entered a growing period [3]. The }
\put(29.64,-445.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}domestic hair loss market consists of hair care products, hair }
\put(29.64,-456.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}care services, hair loss treatments, wigs and hair transplants, }
\put(29.64,-467.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and related new products are being developed one after }
\put(29.64,-478.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}another in the pharmaceutical and household goods }
\put(29.64,-489.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}industries. South Korean firm LG Electronics has also }
\put(29.64,-500.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}launched its hair care product, LG Pra.L Medihair. }
\put(44.064,-517.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In this article, we redefine the scope of development for}
\put(29.64,-528.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} Pra.L Medihair, focusing on the creation of an application }
\put(29.64,-538.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that utilizes an AI model for hair and scalp analysis. This a}
\put(29.64,-549.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}pplication aims to provide users with detailed insights into }
\put(29.64,-560.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the condition of their hair and scalp. In addition, we plan to}
\put(29.64,-571.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} integrate a feature that recommends treatment solutions ba}
\put(29.64,-582.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}sed on the usage of Pra.L Medihair. These treatment solutio}
\put(29.64,-593.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}ns are generated by a trained generative AI, which also ena}
\put(29.64,-604.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}bles interactive chat capabilities, allowing users to receive }

\put(333.07,-307.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enter the authentication code sent to their email. The }
\put(333.07,-318.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}app validates the code, and the sign-up button }
\put(333.07,-329.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}becomes active only if the correct authentication }
\put(333.07,-340.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}code is entered. }
\put(315.07,-357.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}5. Password Hashing: When storing the user's }
\put(333.07,-368.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password in the database, the app employs Flutter's }
\put(333.07,-379.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}crypto encryption library to perform SHA-256 }
\put(333.07,-390.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hashing on the password before storage. Password }
\put(333.07,-401.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hashing enhances security by ensuring that plain-}
\put(333.07,-412.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}text passwords are not stored directly in the }
\put(333.07,-423.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database. }
\put(315.07,-440.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}When the app starts, it displays the login and sign up }
\put(315.07,-451.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen. The User enters their ID and password. The }
\put(315.07,-461.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}entered password is hashed using SHA-256. If this }
\put(315.07,-472.87){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hashed password matches the ID stored in the database, }
\put(315.07,-483.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the app displays ‘Login Successful’ message and }
\put(315.07,-494.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}proceeds to the next screen. If the password is incorrect, }
\put(315.07,-505.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}messages like 'Incorrect password' or 'The entered ID }
\put(315.07,-516.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}does not exist' are displayed. Additionally, provide an }
\put(315.07,-527.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}option for password reset through email verification for }
\put(315.07,-538.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}users who have forgotten their passwords. }
\put(315.07,-555.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-572.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}B. Log in  }
\put(315.07,-586.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1. Initial Screen: When the app is launched, the login }
\put(333.07,-597.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen is displayed to users as the initial interface, }
\put(333.07,-608.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}providing access to existing users. }
\put(315.07,-625.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2. User Input: The user is required to enter their }
\put(333.07,-636.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}credentials, including: }
\put(333.07,-654.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• ID: A unique identifier associated with the user. }
\put(333.07,-671.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• Password: The secret passphrase known only to }
\put(348.91,-682.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the user. }
\put(315.07,-699.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3. Password Hashing: The entered password is }
\put(333.07,-710.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}securely hashed using the SHA-256 hashing }
\put(333.07,-721.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}algorithm before it is compared to the stored hash }
\put(333.07,-732.336){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in the database. Hashing the password enhances }
\put(333.07,-743.256){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}security by ensuring that plain-text passwords are }
\put(333.07,-754.176){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}not transmitted or stored. }

\put(315.07,-447.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2. Data Collection:  }
\put(333.07,-464.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The following data is collected from the user: }

\put(331.87,-591.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Areas Affected by Hair Loss: Users specify }
\put(353.83,-602.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the regions or areas on their scalp or body }
\put(353.83,-613.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}affected by hair loss. This data aids in }
\put(353.83,-624.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}identifying the extent of hair loss. }

\put(76.104,-456.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}III. DEVELOPMENT ENVIRONMENT }
\put(29.64,-474.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}A. Choice of Software Development Platform }
\put(29.64,-488.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Our team is planning to develop a cross-platform }
\put(29.64,-500.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application that will work on both Android and iOS. To }
\put(29.64,-511.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}achieve this, we will utilize the Flutter framework, allowing }
\put(29.64,-523.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}us to build a compatible application for both platforms }
\put(29.64,-534.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}using a single codebase. The backend of the application }
\put(29.64,-546.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}will be developed using Node.js, known for its exceptional }
\put(29.64,-557.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}scalability and data processing capabilities, along with }
\put(29.64,-569.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}support for various modules/libraries that empower }
\put(29.64,-580.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}developers to implement a wide range of functionalities. }
\put(29.64,-592.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Our AI model, built using Scikit-learn, will leverage }

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(29.64,-226.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(29.64,-243.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}B. Cost Estimation }
\put(39.6,-258.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}To ensure the successful development and functionality }
\put(29.64,-269.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of our application, it is crucial to establish a seamless flow }
\put(29.64,-281.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of data between the server and the database while }
\put(29.64,-292.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}maintaining real-time communication. To achieve this, we }
\put(29.64,-304.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}have chosen to leverage Amazon's EC2 (Elastic Compute }
\put(29.64,-315.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Cloud) as our server hosting solution. While it's true that }
\put(29.64,-327.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hosting on EC2 incurs costs, the advantages it offers are }
\put(29.64,-338.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}instrumental to our application's performance and }
\put(29.64,-350.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}reliability. }
\put(34.68,-361.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(39.6,-373.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}One of the key benefits of utilizing Amazon EC2 is its }
\put(29.64,-384.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}scalability. EC2 allows us to easily scale our application's }
\put(29.64,-396.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}resources up or down to accommodate varying workloads }
\put(29.64,-407.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and user demands. This scalability ensures that our }
\put(29.64,-419.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application remains responsive and efficient, even during }
\put(29.64,-430.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}peak usage periods. Additionally, EC2 provides a high }
\put(29.64,-442.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}level of reliability and availability, which are critical for }
\put(29.64,-453.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}our application's uptime and data accessibility. }
\put(34.68,-465.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(39.6,-476.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In addition to hosting, we are integrating multiple APIs }
\put(29.64,-488.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}into our system to access database information and live }
\put(29.64,-499.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server updates. This approach not only enhances data }
\put(29.64,-511.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}retrieval but also keeps our application's information up-}
\put(29.64,-522.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to-date, contributing to an improved overall user }
\put(29.64,-534.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}experience. The combination of Amazon EC2's }
\put(29.64,-545.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}scalability, reliability, and the integration of these APIs }

\put(300.67,-514.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}support for handling large, multi-dimensional arrays and }
\put(300.67,-525.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}matrices, along with a comprehensive collection of }
\put(300.67,-535.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}mathematical functions. These capabilities are crucial for }
\put(300.67,-546.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}our data preprocessing, mathematical computations, and }
\put(300.67,-557.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}data analysis tasks within the project. NumPy's efficiency }
\put(300.67,-568.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and performance advantages over native Python lists make }
\put(300.67,-579.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it the ideal choice for working with large datasets, ensuring }
\put(300.67,-590.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that our data science team can process and analyze data }
\put(300.67,-601.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}efficiently. Additionally, NumPy integrates seamlessly with }
\put(300.67,-612.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}other scientific computing libraries, such as SciPy and }
\put(300.67,-623.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}matplotlib, further expanding our capabilities for advanced }
\put(300.67,-634.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}data analysis and visualization. In summary, NumPy forms }
\put(300.67,-645.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the backbone of our data science and numerical computing }
\put(300.67,-656.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}workflows, enabling us to perform complex calculations }
\put(300.67,-667.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and manipulations effectively.[18] }
\put(315.07,-683.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }

\put(29.64,-199.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}A. Login Page }
\put(44.064,-213.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The login page consists of the following components: an }
\put(29.64,-224.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}'email input field,' a 'password input field,' a 'login button,' a }
\put(29.64,-235.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}'forgot password button,' and a 'sign-up button.' The email }
\put(29.64,-246.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}input field has a maximum length limitation of 20 characters. }
\put(29.64,-256.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The password input field must be between 10 and 20 }
\put(29.64,-267.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}characters in length, and it must contain both English letters }
\put(29.64,-278.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and numbers, with the option to include special characters. }
\put(44.064,-295.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}When a user enters their email and password and clicks }
\put(29.64,-306.65){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the login button, the system first checks if the email and }
\put(29.64,-317.57){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password meet the specified rules. Subsequently, the login }
\put(29.64,-328.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}API is invoked, sending the email and the SHA-256 hashed }
\put(29.64,-339.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password to the server. }
\put(44.064,-356.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Within the login API, if the email and the SHA-256 }
\put(29.64,-367.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hashed password match records in the database, a successful }
\put(29.64,-378.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}login message is sent along with a token containing the }
\put(29.64,-389.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user's information to the page. Upon receiving the }
\put(29.64,-400.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}successful login message, the user is redirected to the next }
\put(29.64,-410.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}page using the provided token. }
\put(44.064,-427.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In cases where the email and hashed password do not }
\put(29.64,-438.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}match any records in the database, the login API sends a }
\put(29.64,-449.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}login failure message to the page. Upon receiving the login }
\put(29.64,-460.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}failure message, the system displays the message to the user, }
\put(29.64,-471.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}indicating that the login attempt was unsuccessful. }
\put(44.064,-488.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Additionally, the login page offers buttons for users who }
\put(29.64,-499.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}have forgotten their passwords and those who need to sign }
\put(29.64,-510.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}up for a new account, allowing them to navigate to the }
\put(29.64,-521.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}'forgot password' and 'sign-up' pages, respectively. }
\put(44.064,-538.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(29.64,-555.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}B. Register page }
\put(44.064,-569.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Email-Based Registration: Users opting for traditional }
\put(29.64,-580.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}email-based registration are required to enter their email }
\put(29.64,-591.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}address. Upon submission, a verification code is sent to the }
\put(29.64,-602.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}provided email address. The 'verify code' button remains }
\put(29.64,-613.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}active for a duration of three minutes after sending the email. }
\put(60.864,-630.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Email addresses must be under 20 characters }
\put(82.824,-641.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in length to meet system requirements. }
\put(60.864,-658.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Once the correct verification code is entered, }
\put(82.824,-669.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the 'sign-up' button becomes active, allowing }
\put(82.824,-680.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}users to proceed. }
\put(60.864,-696.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Users are prompted to enter their chosen }
\put(82.824,-707.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password twice for verification. Passwords }
\put(82.824,-718.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}must adhere to the same criteria mentioned }
\put(82.824,-729.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}earlier, which include a combination of }
\put(82.824,-740.616){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}English letters and numbers, a length between }
\put(82.824,-751.536){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}10 and 15 characters, and the option to include }
\put(353.83,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}special characters. The double entry of the }
\put(353.83,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password helps ensure its accuracy. }
\put(331.87,-79.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- If the verification code is correct and the }
\put(353.83,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password meets the specified criteria, the }
\put(353.83,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user's email and password details are securely }
\put(353.83,-112.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}stored in the database, with the password }
\put(353.83,-123.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}being hashed using the SHA-256 encryption }
\put(353.83,-134.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}method. }
\put(300.67,-151.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This comprehensive registration process provides users with }
\put(300.67,-162.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}flexibility and security, accommodating various preferences }
\put(300.67,-173.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}while maintaining the necessary security measures. }
\put(300.67,-190.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}C. User Information Entry Page }
\put(315.07,-204.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This page collects the user's name, age, gender, and }
\put(300.67,-215.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}nickname. Names must be under 5 characters in Korean. }
\put(300.67,-226.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Age is a two-digit integer. Gender selection is configured as }
\put(300.67,-237.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}either male or female. Nicknames are set to under 10 }
\put(300.67,-248.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}characters and can consist of Korean, English, or numbers. }
\put(300.67,-259.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The information collected is stored in the database. The }
\put(300.67,-270.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}entered age and gender are used to compare with the average }
\put(300.67,-281.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hair thickness and density for that gender and age to assess }
\put(300.67,-292.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the user's hair loss condition. }
\put(315.07,-309.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }

\put(29.64,-168.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}E. Hair Analysis Page }
\put(44.064,-182.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}On the 'Hair Analysis' page, users have the capability to }
\put(29.64,-193.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}take photos of their hair and perform an analysis. These }
\put(29.64,-204.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}photos can be captured using a mobile phone camera, but }
\put(29.64,-215.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}for enhanced accuracy, users are encouraged to utilize a }
\put(29.64,-226.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}digital electronic microscope. }
\put(29.64,-243.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} While the analysis is in progress, a demonstration video }
\put(29.64,-254.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}showcasing the operation of the MediHair product is }
\put(29.64,-265.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}displayed to the user. }
\put(29.64,-282.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} Once the user submits the captured photos, these images }
\put(29.64,-293.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}are transmitted to the hair analysis AI model via an API. The }
\put(29.64,-304.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}AI model then processes the user-provided images and }
\put(29.64,-315.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}derives the following information: }
\put(60.864,-331.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Type of Hair Loss: The specific type of hair }
\put(82.824,-342.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}loss the user is experiencing }
\put(60.864,-359.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Density: The user's hair density (e.g., 13 }
\put(82.824,-370.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}per 1cm²). }
\put(60.864,-387.65){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Thickness: The diameter of the user's hair }
\put(82.824,-398.57){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}strands (e.g., 45μm). }
\put(44.064,-415.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The server retrieves this data and securely stores it in the }
\put(29.64,-426.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database, simultaneously sending the information to be }
\put(29.64,-437.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}displayed on the page. The types and data formats stored in }
\put(29.64,-448.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the database include: }
\put(60.864,-465.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Analysis Date (in yyyy-mm-dd format) }
\put(60.864,-482.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Loss Status (varchar(5)) }
\put(60.864,-499.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Severity of Hair Loss (varchar(5)) }
\put(60.864,-515.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Thickness (float type) }
\put(60.864,-532.87){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Density (int type) }
\put(44.064,-549.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The AI model presents the analyzed results to the user }
\put(29.64,-560.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and recommends an appropriate treatment mode based on }
\put(29.64,-571.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the findings (e.g., front mode). Additionally, any further }
\put(29.64,-582.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}details or recommendations from the analysis can be }
\put(29.64,-593.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}included as needed. }
\put(44.064,-610.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This comprehensive process empowers users to gain }
\put(29.64,-621.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}insights into their hair health and receive personalized }
\put(29.64,-632.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}treatment recommendations for their specific hair loss }
\put(29.64,-643.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}condition. }
\put(44.064,-660.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }

\put(82.824,-490.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}clutter-free alarm setup. }
\put(60.864,-507.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Set Specific Dates and Times: Users have the }
\put(82.824,-518.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}freedom to customize each alarm by }
\put(82.824,-529.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}specifying particular dates and times for their }
\put(82.824,-540.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Medihair usage reminders. }
\put(44.064,-557.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This user-friendly interface streamlines the process of }
\put(29.64,-568.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}setting and managing alarms, ensuring that users receive }
\put(29.64,-579.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}timely reminders for their Medi-hair usage. These alarms }
\put(29.64,-589.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}play a crucial role in helping users monitor and maintain }
\put(29.64,-600.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}their hair health effectively over time. }
\put(29.64,-618.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(29.64,-635.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}J. Profile }
\put(44.064,-649.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}On the profile management page, users can log in and }
\put(29.64,-660.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}log out. Pressing the logout button takes the user back to the }
\put(29.64,-671.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}initial login screen. Additionally, the option to add a new }
\put(29.64,-682.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}profile is provided, allowing each profile to have a unique }
\put(29.64,-693.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}nickname. Clicking the button to add a new user prompts }
\put(29.64,-704.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the user to enter their name, age, gender, and nickname. }
\put(29.64,-715.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Names must be five characters or less and composed of }
\put(29.64,-726.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Korean characters. Age is a two-digit integer. Gender }
\put(29.64,-737.256){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}options are set to be selectable between male and female. }
\put(29.64,-748.176){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Nicknames are set to be 10 characters or less and can be }
\put(300.67,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}composed of Korean, English, and numerals. The }
\put(300.67,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}information of the new user, such as name, age, gender, and }
\put(300.67,-73.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}nickname, is added to the User\_Info table corresponding to }
\put(300.67,-84.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the user's email in the database. The number of users per }
\put(300.67,-95.65997){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}email is limited to four. If there are more than two users, the }
\put(300.67,-106.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}app's start page will allow the selection of a user's name to }
\put(300.67,-117.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}begin using the app. The feature provides flexibility in }
\put(300.67,-128.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}switching users, allowing users to easily switch between }
\put(300.67,-139.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}profiles and personalize their experience on the platform.  }
\put(315.07,-156.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-173.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(333.55,-192.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}V. ARCHITECTURE DESIGN \& IMPLEMENT  }
\put(300.67,-208.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}A. Overall Architecture }
\put(538.06,-363.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(359.11,-378.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Figure 1. Overall Architecture }
\put(418.15,-390.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-401.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook Sook application is structured into four main }
\put(300.67,-412.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}architectural components: }
\put(315.07,-429.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) App Frontend: The frontend of the application is }
\put(337.03,-440.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}developed using Flutter. Flutter is chosen for its }
\put(337.03,-451.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}versatility, allowing developers to write code once }
\put(337.03,-462.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and deploy it on both iOS and Android platforms. }
\put(337.03,-473.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This cross-platform compatibility significantly }
\put(337.03,-484.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}reduces development effort and time. Additionally, }
\put(337.03,-495.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Flutter offers a rich set of libraries and widgets that }
\put(337.03,-506.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enable the implementation of various features and }
\put(337.03,-517.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user interface elements, enhancing the user }
\put(337.03,-527.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}experience. }
\put(315.07,-544.87){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) App Backend: The backend of the application is }
\put(337.03,-555.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}built using Node.js. Node.js is selected for its ease }
\put(337.03,-566.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of learning, as it uses JavaScript, a widely-known }
\put(337.03,-577.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}programming language. Node.js also provides }
\put(337.03,-588.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}access to a vast ecosystem of modules and libraries, }
\put(337.03,-599.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}including MySQL for database interactions and }
\put(337.03,-610.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Nodemailer for email-related functionalities. The }
\put(337.03,-621.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}decision to use Node.js is driven by its ability to }
\put(337.03,-632.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}handle asynchronous tasks efficiently, making it }
\put(337.03,-643.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}well-suited for building responsive and scalable }
\put(337.03,-654.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server-side applications. }
\put(352.99,-671.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The server is hosted on an Amazon Web }
\put(333.07,-682.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Services (AWS) EC2 environment, enabling the }
\put(333.07,-692.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}setup of a domain and allowing external access to }
\put(333.07,-703.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the application. AWS EC2 provides scalable }
\put(333.07,-714.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}compute capacity, and the use of this cloud }
\put(333.07,-725.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environment ensures that the application can handle }
\put(333.07,-736.656){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}v}
\put(315.05,-363.02){\includegraphics[width=222.52pt,height=152.85pt]{latexImage_4de49e2c1df6c00f408d4dd36b859f6d.png}}
\end{picture}

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(277.73,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}13 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(62.064,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}availability. It also allows for easy scaling as the }
\put(62.064,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user base grows. }
\put(44.064,-79.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3) Database (DB): MySQL is chosen as the relational }
\put(66.024,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database management system (RDBMS) for the }
\put(66.024,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook Sook application. MySQL is well-suited for }
\put(66.024,-112.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}this application for several reasons:  }
\put(60.864,-129.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Structured Data: MySQL excels at managing }
\put(82.824,-140.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}structured data, which is crucial for storing }
\put(82.824,-151.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user information, hair-related data, and other }
\put(82.824,-162.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}structured records. }
\put(60.864,-179.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Data Integrity: MySQL ensures data integrity }
\put(82.824,-190.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}through features like constraints, foreign keys, }
\put(82.824,-201.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and transactions, ensuring that the data }
\put(82.824,-211.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}remains accurate and consistent. }
\put(60.864,-228.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Query Capabilities: MySQL offers powerful }
\put(82.824,-239.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}querying capabilities, enabling efficient }
\put(82.824,-250.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}retrieval and analysis of data. }
\put(54.024,-267.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The application's MySQL database is hosted on AWS }
\put(44.064,-278.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}RDS (Relational Database Service), which provides }
\put(44.064,-289.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}managed database services. AWS RDS handles }
\put(44.064,-300.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database administration tasks such as backups, software }
\put(44.064,-311.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}patching, and scaling, allowing the development team to }
\put(44.064,-322.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}focus on application development. }
\put(44.064,-339.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}4) ML Backend: The machine learning (ML) }
\put(66.024,-350.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}backend utilized the efficientnet-b0 library for ML }
\put(66.024,-361.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model development, leveraging Transfer Learning }
\put(66.024,-372.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}capabilities. Three AI models were constructed for }
\put(66.024,-382.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the application: }
\put(60.864,-399.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Loss Type and Severity Analysis Model: }
\put(82.824,-410.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This model helps classify and assess the }
\put(82.824,-421.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}severity of hair loss based on input data. It }
\put(82.824,-432.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}assists users in understanding their hair loss }
\put(82.824,-443.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}condition. }
\put(60.864,-460.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Thickness Analysis Model: This model }
\put(82.824,-471.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analyzes hair thickness, providing insights }
\put(82.824,-482.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}into the user's hair characteristics. }
\put(60.864,-499.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Hair Density Analysis Model: This model }
\put(82.824,-510.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}evaluates hair density, which is valuable }
\put(82.824,-521.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}information for understanding the user's hair }
\put(82.824,-532.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}health. }
\put(44.064,-548.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} Google Colab is chosen for its accessibility and }
\put(44.064,-559.87){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}ease of use in the machine learning field. It provides a }
\put(44.064,-570.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}cloud-based environment with pre-installed libraries, }
\put(44.064,-581.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}making it convenient for ML model development }
\put(44.064,-592.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}without the need for extensive setup. Additionally, }
\put(44.064,-603.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Google Colab offers GPU support, accelerating the }
\put(44.064,-614.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}training of machine learning models. }
\put(29.64,-631.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-648.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In summary, the architectural choices made for the Sook }
\put(29.64,-659.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook application are driven by the need for versatility, ease }
\put(29.64,-670.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of development, scalability, data integrity, and efficient }
\put(29.64,-681.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}machine learning model development. These components }
\put(29.64,-692.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}work together to create a robust and user-friendly }
\put(29.64,-703.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application that provides valuable insights into hair health }
\put(29.64,-713.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and related information. }
\put(536.14,-204.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(381.91,-220.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Figure 2.Database }
\put(300.67,-231.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The backend server is implemented using Node.js and is }
\put(300.67,-242.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}executed through Express. It connects to the MySQL }
\put(300.67,-253.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database using the Node.js MySQL library. To achieve this, }
\put(300.67,-264.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the necessary database connection information is stored in }
\put(300.67,-275.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a .env file and retrieved as follows: }

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(300.67,-411.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-428.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The choice of Node.js for the backend server is made for }
\put(300.67,-439.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}several reasons. Node.js is known for its non-blocking, }
\put(300.67,-450.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}event-driven architecture, making it highly scalable and }
\put(300.67,-461.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}efficient for handling asynchronous tasks, which is crucial }
\put(300.67,-472.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in web applications. Express is a popular web application }
\put(300.67,-483.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}framework for Node.js, offering a robust set of features and }
\put(300.67,-494.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}middleware for building RESTful APIs and web services. }
\put(300.67,-505.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}These technologies enable us to build a fast and responsive }
\put(300.67,-516.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}backend server that can handle a high volume of requests }
\put(300.67,-526.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and database interactions. }
\put(315.07,-543.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1. Sook Sook’s application uses MySQL as its database }
\put(300.67,-554.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}system to store data. The decision to use a relational }
\put(300.67,-565.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database like MySQL is driven by the need to manage }
\put(300.67,-576.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}structured data and relationships efficiently. Relational }
\put(300.67,-587.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}databases provide data integrity, consistency, and support }
\put(300.67,-598.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}for complex queries, making them suitable for applications }
\put(300.67,-609.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that involve data with well-defined structures and }
\put(300.67,-620.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}associations. }
\put(315.07,-637.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2. User's hair loss information, including hair density, }
\put(300.67,-648.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}thickness, loss type, scalp condition, hair age, date, user }
\put(300.67,-659.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}email, and times, is stored in the Hair\_history table. The }
\put(300.67,-670.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}choice of using a separate table for hair loss information }
\put(300.67,-680.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}allows for organized data storage and efficient querying }
\put(300.67,-691.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}based on specific attributes. This structured approach makes }
\put(300.67,-702.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it easier to analyze and retrieve hair-related data for user }
\put(300.67,-713.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}profiles and assessments. }
\put(315.07,-730.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3. During the registration process, user information is }
\put(300.67,-741.696){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}stored in the Customer\_Info table. The Customer\_Info table }
\put(300.67,-752.616){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in}
\put(300.65,-203.91){\includegraphics[width=235pt,height=161.4pt]{latexImage_5e6721869688fd34ddd5f43c5a15f89c.png}}
\end{picture}

\begin{tikzpicture}[overlay]\path(0pt,0pt);\end{tikzpicture}
\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(277.73,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}14 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(29.64,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Storing user registration information separately provides }
\put(29.64,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}security and access control, ensuring that sensitive data such }
\put(29.64,-73.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}as passwords are properly protected. }
\put(44.064,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}4. After registration, the initial user information is stored }
\put(29.64,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in the User\_Info table. This information includes the user's }
\put(29.64,-112.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}name, email, age, sex, and nickname. Additionally, this }
\put(29.64,-123.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}table is used to assess the user's hair loss severity by }
\put(29.64,-134.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}comparing it to the average hair loss severity for their age }
\put(29.64,-145.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}group. Storing this information separately enables }
\put(29.64,-156.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}personalized assessments and recommendations based on }
\put(29.64,-167.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the user's profile and hair loss status. }
\put(44.064,-184.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}5. All backend components are deployed on the Amazon }
\put(29.64,-195.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}SWeb Service (AWS) cloud computing platform. The main }
\put(29.64,-205.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server and the second server are deployed on separate AWS }
\put(29.64,-216.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Elastic Compute Cloud (EC2) instances, while the database }
\put(29.64,-227.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}is hosted on AWS Relational Database Service (RDS). This }
\put(29.64,-238.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}cloud-based deployment offers scalability, reliability, and }
\put(29.64,-249.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}accessibility, ensuring that the application can handle }
\put(29.64,-260.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}varying workloads and provide high availability to users. }
\put(29.64,-277.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} 6. The use of AWS services, such as EC2 and RDS, }
\put(29.64,-288.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}offers various advantages, including automatic scaling, data }
\put(29.64,-299.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}backup, and security features. AWS's infrastructure-as-a-}
\put(29.64,-310.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}service (IaaS) and database-as-a-service (DBaaS) offerings }
\put(29.64,-321.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}simplify the management and maintenance of the backend }
\put(29.64,-332.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}components, allowing the development team to focus on }
\put(29.64,-343.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}building and enhancing the application's features and }
\put(29.64,-354.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}functionality. }
\put(109.82,-371.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Table IV: Database }
\put(35.28,-383.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Table name Column name (Datatype) }
\put(213.17,-382.85){\fontsize{9}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Constraints }

\put(44.064,-756.936){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-52.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}C.  Modules }
\put(315.07,-69.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1. Front-end }
\put(315.07,-84.02002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a. Purpose }
\put(315.07,-100.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}To develop Sook Sook, we used Flutter so that a it can }
\put(300.67,-111.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}be used in a cross-platform for both Android and iOS }
\put(300.67,-122.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environment. Frontend serves as a role in providing }
\put(300.67,-133.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}interface to a user. It connects user and server by providing }
\put(300.67,-144.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}input fields that a user can enter information. Once this job }
\put(300.67,-155.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}is done, the values are delivered to backend. Also, Frontend }
\put(300.67,-166.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}brings data in the database and provides it to the user after }
\put(300.67,-177.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}changing it to a data that a user can understand. }
\put(315.07,-194.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}b. Functionality }
\put(315.07,-211.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook Sook application, developed using Flutter, }
\put(300.67,-222.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}encompasses a wide range of features for comprehensive }
\put(300.67,-233.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user engagement. It begins with a robust login page, }
\put(300.67,-243.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}ensuring secure access with stringent criteria for email and }
\put(300.67,-254.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}password inputs. Users can also navigate to the 'Forgot }
\put(300.67,-265.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Password' and 'Sign-up' pages for account recovery and }
\put(300.67,-276.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}registration, respectively. The registration process is email-}
\put(300.67,-287.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}based, featuring email verification and secure password }
\put(300.67,-298.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}storage. The User Information Entry page collects essential }
\put(300.67,-309.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}personal data for tailored hair loss assessment. The Main }
\put(300.67,-320.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Page offers various functionalities, including hair analysis, }
\put(300.67,-331.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}record reviews, chatbot interaction, access to a hair loss }
\put(300.67,-342.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}community, and product integration. The Hair Analysis }
\put(300.67,-353.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Page enables users to capture and analyze hair images, }
\put(300.67,-364.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}receiving personalized recommendations based on the }
\put(300.67,-375.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}results. Users can review their analysis records on the Hair }
\put(300.67,-386.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Record Page. The Settings section offers connection status }
\put(300.67,-397.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}checks, manuals, and dark mode. The Alarm Page facilitates }
\put(300.67,-407.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}alarm management for timely Medihair usage reminders. }
\put(300.67,-418.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Profile management allows multiple user profiles, }
\put(300.67,-429.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enhancing personalization. These features collectively }
\put(300.67,-440.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}provide a comprehensive and user-friendly platform for hair }
\put(300.67,-451.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}health management and treatment. }
