\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(277.73,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}17 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-52.67999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• lib/analysisloding.dart  }
\put(44.064,-69.59998){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(67.824,-86.53998){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- import 'package:flutter/material.dart'; }
\put(67.824,-103.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This library is used to import Flutter's UI }
\put(67.824,-114.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}components and Material Design for building the }
\put(67.824,-125.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user interface. It's essential for creating the visual }
\put(67.824,-136.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}elements and structure of the app. }
\put(60.864,-153.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- import 'dart:async'; }
\put(77.904,-170.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The Dart async library is imported to handle }
\put(77.904,-180.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}asynchronous operations. In this code, it's used }
\put(77.904,-191.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to implement a timer for delaying the execution }
\put(77.904,-202.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of a function. }
\put(60.864,-219.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- import 'dart:convert'; }
\put(77.904,-236.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The Dart convert library is imported for }
\put(77.904,-247.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}encoding and decoding JSON data. In this code, }
\put(77.904,-258.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it's used to encode the data before sending it to }
\put(77.904,-269.57){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a server. }
\put(60.864,-286.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- import 'package:http/http.dart' as http; }
\put(77.904,-303.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This library is imported to make HTTP requests }
\put(77.904,-314.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to a remote server. It's used to send data to the }
\put(77.904,-325.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server and handle the server's response. }
\put(60.864,-342.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- 'analysisresult.dart'; }
\put(77.904,-359.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This import references another Dart file, likely }
\put(77.904,-370.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}defining the Analysisresult widget, which is }
\put(77.904,-380.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}used to display analysis results. It enables code }
\put(77.904,-391.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}modularity and separation of concerns. }
\put(44.064,-408.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code Functionality: }
\put(60.864,-425.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Analysisloding is a StatefulWidget that }
\put(82.824,-436.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}represents a loading screen during a data }
\put(82.824,-447.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analysis or processing task. It receives the }
\put(82.824,-458.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}user's email, one, and two as parameters. }
\put(60.864,-475.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- initState(): This method is called when the }
\put(82.824,-486.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}widget is initialized. It sets a 4-second timer }
\put(82.824,-497.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that, when elapsed, calls the sendHairAnalysis }
\put(82.824,-508.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}function. The purpose of this delay is to }
\put(82.824,-519.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}simulate a loading screen before sending data }
\put(82.824,-529.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to a server. }
\put(60.864,-546.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- sendHairAnalysis(): This asynchronous }
\put(82.824,-557.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}function sends a POST request to a server at a }
\put(82.824,-568.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}specified URL, passing the user's email, one, }
\put(82.824,-579.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and two as JSON data. If the server responds }
\put(82.824,-590.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}with a status code of 200 (success), it }
\put(82.824,-601.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}navigates the user to the Analysisresult widget }
\put(82.824,-612.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to display the analysis results. Otherwise, it }
\put(82.824,-623.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}handles the error by printing the server's status }
\put(82.824,-634.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}code. }
\put(60.864,-651.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- build(): This method is responsible for }
\put(82.824,-662.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}building the widget's UI. The UI consists of a }
\put(82.824,-673.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}black background (Colors.black87) with an }
\put(82.824,-684.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}animated GIF displayed on top. The }
\put(82.824,-695.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Image.asset widget loads a GIF image, and it's }
\put(82.824,-705.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}positioned using a Stack with Positioned }
\put(82.824,-716.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}widgets to create the loading animation effect. }
\put(44.064,-733.776){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-750.696){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3) Code Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-68.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The primary purpose of this code is to create }
\put(353.83,-79.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}an "Analysisloding" widget, which serves as a }
\put(353.83,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}loading screen during data analysis. It visually }
\put(353.83,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}indicates to the user that the app is actively }
\put(353.83,-112.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}working on a task. After a 4-second delay, it }
\put(353.83,-123.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}automatically sends user data to a remote }
\put(353.83,-134.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server for analysis. Upon successful analysis, }
\put(353.83,-145.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it navigates the user to the Analysisresult }
\put(353.83,-156.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}widget to display the results. This loading }
\put(353.83,-167.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen enhances the user experience by }
\put(353.83,-178.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}providing visual feedback during potentially }
\put(353.83,-189.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}time-consuming operations and separates the }
\put(353.83,-199.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analysis logic from the UI logic for }

\put(44.064,-447.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(60.864,-464.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- dart:async: This Dart library is used for }
\put(82.824,-475.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}working with asynchronous operations. In this }
\put(82.824,-486.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}code, it's used to create a delay (4 seconds) }
\put(82.824,-497.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}before navigating to the login page. }
\put(60.864,-514.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- loginpage.dart: This is a user-defined module }
\put(82.824,-525.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}(assumed to be part of your Flutter project) }
\put(82.824,-535.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that likely contains the login page widget. It's }
\put(82.824,-546.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}imported so that the application can navigate }
\put(82.824,-557.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to it when the splash screen is done. }
\put(44.064,-574.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code Functionality: }
\put(60.864,-591.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- This code creates a Flutter widget called }
\put(82.824,-602.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}"SplashScreen," which serves as the initial }
\put(82.824,-613.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen displayed when the app is launched. }
\put(60.864,-630.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Inside the initState method, a Timer is set to }
\put(82.824,-641.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}wait for 4 seconds. After this delay, it }
\put(82.824,-652.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}navigates to the login page using }
\put(82.824,-663.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Navigator.pushReplacement. }
\put(60.864,-680.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The Navigator.pushReplacement method }
\put(82.824,-691.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}replaces the current screen (the splash screen) }
\put(82.824,-702.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}with the login page, ensuring that users cannot }
\put(82.824,-713.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}navigate back to the splash screen using the }
\put(82.824,-723.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}back button. }
\put(82.824,-740.856){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3) Code Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-68.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The purpose of this code is to create a splash }
\put(353.83,-79.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen for the app, which is typically used to }
\put(353.83,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}display a loading indicator, logo, or any other }
\put(353.83,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}introductory content when the app is launched. }
\put(331.87,-118.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The splash screen provides a smooth transition }
\put(353.83,-129.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to the main content of the app, in this case, the }
\put(353.83,-140.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}login page. }
\put(331.87,-157.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- By delaying the navigation to the login page, }
\put(353.83,-168.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it gives the impression of a brief introduction }
\put(353.83,-179.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}or branding display before users access the }
\put(353.83,-190.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}app's core functionality. }
\put(347.47,-207.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In summary, this code is designed to create a }
\put(333.07,-217.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}splash screen that briefly appears when the app is }
\put(333.07,-228.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}launched, and after a 4-second delay, it }
\put(333.07,-239.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}automatically navigates the user to the login page. }
\put(333.07,-250.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The purpose is to enhance the user experience and }
\put(333.07,-261.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}provide a polished entry point to the app. }

\put(315.07,-313.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-330.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- package:flutter/material.dart }
\put(353.83,-347.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} This is the core Flutter framework library for }
\put(353.83,-358.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}building user interfaces. It's used to create the }
\put(353.83,-368.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}visual components and structure of the login }
\put(353.83,-379.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}screen. }
\put(331.87,-396.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- package:http/http.dart as http }
\put(353.83,-413.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This library is used to make HTTP requests to }
\put(353.83,-424.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a remote server for user authentication and }
\put(353.83,-435.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}login. }
\put(331.87,-452.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- dart:convert }
\put(353.83,-469.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}It's used for encoding and decoding JSON data, }
\put(353.83,-480.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}which is commonly used in communication }
\put(353.83,-491.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}between the Flutter app and a server. }
\put(331.87,-508.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- dart:async }
\put(353.83,-525.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This Dart library is used for handling }
\put(353.83,-535.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}asynchronous operations such as setting }
\put(353.83,-546.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}timers for delayed actions. }
\put(331.87,-563.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- legistrationscreen.dart, findpassword.dart, }
\put(353.83,-574.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analysispage.dart, recordpage.dart, }
\put(353.83,-585.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}chatpage.dart: These are user-defined modules }
\put(353.83,-596.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}(assumed to be part of your Flutter project) }
\put(353.83,-607.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}that contain various screens or components }
\put(353.83,-618.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}used for navigation. }
\put(315.07,-635.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code Functionality: }
\put(331.87,-652.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- This code creates a Flutter widget called }
\put(353.83,-663.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}"LogIn," which represents the login screen of }
\put(353.83,-674.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the application. }

\put(44.064,-150.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a. Purpose }
\put(58.464,-167.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The backend is responsible for managing servers and }
\put(44.064,-178.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}databases. It stores and manages data, as well as handles }
\put(44.064,-189.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}actions taken by users on the client side of the }
\put(44.064,-200.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application. The backend's roles include storing data }
\put(44.064,-211.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}generated as a result of user behavior in the frontend }
\put(44.064,-222.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database (Front Desk) and retrieving data required by }
\put(44.064,-233.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}users from the frontend database (Front Desk). }
\put(58.464,-250.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook Sook chose to implement the backend using }
\put(44.064,-261.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Node.js and MySQL. Node.js was chosen due to its }
\put(44.064,-271.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}extensive selection of modules, offering a wide range of }
\put(44.064,-282.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}functionalities for implementation. MySQL, a relational }
\put(44.064,-293.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database, was selected for its ability to organize data into }
\put(44.064,-304.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}tables }
\put(44.064,-321.65){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}b. Functionality }
\put(58.464,-338.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Sook Sook's application uses an AI model for }
\put(44.064,-349.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analyzing the condition of hair loss and scalp health, and }
\put(44.064,-360.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it stores the extracted results in a database. The backend }
\put(44.064,-371.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}server comes into play during the process of sending }
\put(44.064,-382.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}photos to the server and storing the extracted results in }
\put(44.064,-393.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the database. Additionally, it provides functionality to }
\put(44.064,-404.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}check the analysis results on a daily basis, which }
\put(44.064,-415.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}involves retrieving data from the database and sending }
\put(44.064,-426.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it to the frontend. Other key features include login, user }
\put(44.064,-436.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}registration, fetching analyzed dates, record verification, }
\put(44.064,-447.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and comparing analysis results on a daily basis.3. }

\put(82.824,-611.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In a Node.js project, the package.json file }
\put(82.824,-622.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}serves as a configuration file that contains }
\put(82.824,-633.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}project details, script commands, and }
\put(82.824,-644.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}dependency information, allowing developers }
\put(82.824,-655.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to define the project's settings, including the }
\put(82.824,-666.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}required external packages and their versions. }
\put(82.824,-677.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}On the other hand, the package-lock.json file }
\put(82.824,-687.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}is generated automatically and provides a }
\put(82.824,-698.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}detailed record of the project's dependency }
\put(82.824,-709.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}tree, specifying the exact versions of packages }
\put(82.824,-720.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and their interdependencies. It ensures }
\put(82.824,-731.736){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}consistency and reproducibility by enabling }
\put(82.824,-742.656){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}precise package version control during project }
\put(353.83,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}replication or deployment in different }
\put(353.83,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environments. }
\put(315.07,-80.53998){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• app.js  }
\put(315.07,-97.46002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-114.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- express: Express.js is a popular web }
\put(353.83,-125.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application framework for Node.js. It is used }
\put(353.83,-136.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to create the server and handle routing, making }
\put(353.83,-147.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it easier to build web APIs and applications. }
\put(331.87,-164.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- body-parser: The body-parser middleware is }
\put(353.83,-174.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}used to parse incoming request bodies in }
\put(353.83,-185.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}JSON format. It's essential for handling JSON }
\put(353.83,-196.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}data sent in HTTP requests. }
\put(331.87,-213.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- mysql: The mysql library is used to establish a }
\put(353.83,-224.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}connection to a MySQL database. It allows the }
\put(353.83,-235.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}application to interact with and query the }
\put(353.83,-246.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database. }
\put(331.87,-263.57){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- config: The config module is likely used to }
\put(353.83,-274.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}store configuration settings for the application, }
\put(353.83,-285.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}such as database connection details and other }
\put(353.83,-296.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environment-specific configurations. }
\put(315.07,-313.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code's Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-330.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The code establishes a connection to a }
\put(353.83,-341.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}MySQL database using the provided }
\put(353.83,-352.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}configuration. }
\put(331.87,-368.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The code defines various routes and uses }
\put(353.83,-379.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}separate route files (e.g., loginRoute, }
\put(353.83,-390.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}sendVerificationRoute, etc.) for each route to }
\put(353.83,-401.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}handle specific API endpoints. }
\put(333.07,-418.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-436.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• routes/Choosen\_date.js }
\put(315.07,-453.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-470.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- mysql: The mysql library is employed to }
\put(353.83,-481.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}establish a connection to a MySQL database }
\put(353.83,-491.95){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and execute SQL queries against it. }
\put(331.87,-508.87){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- config: The config module stores }
\put(353.83,-519.79){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}configuration settings, likely including }
\put(353.83,-530.71){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}database connection details, separately from }
\put(353.83,-541.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the code. }
\put(315.07,-558.55){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code's Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-575.47){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- This code handles HTTP POST requests at the }
\put(353.83,-586.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}root route ('/'). }
\put(331.87,-603.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- It expects the user's email and a specific date }
\put(353.83,-614.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}as inputs in the request body. }
\put(331.87,-631.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The code constructs an SQL query to select }
\put(353.83,-642.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hair-related data (density, thickness, etc.) for }
\put(353.83,-653.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the given user (U\_email) and date from the }
\put(353.83,-664.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}'Hair\_history' table. }
\put(331.87,-680.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Additionally, it queries the 'User\_Info' table to }
\put(353.83,-691.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}retrieve the user's name based on their email. }
\put(331.87,-708.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The code executes these SQL queries, handles }
\put(353.83,-719.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}potential errors, and responds with the }
\put(353.83,-730.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}requested data and the user's name in JSON }
\put(353.83,-741.576){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}format. }
\end{picture}

\put(44.064,-280.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Upon executing the query, it handles potential }
\put(62.064,-291.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}errors and returns the distinct dates as an array in }
\put(62.064,-302.33){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}ISO date format ('YYYY-MM-DD') to the client. }
\put(44.064,-319.25){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-336.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• routes/Get\_Nickname.js }
\put(44.064,-353.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(60.864,-370.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- express: Express.js is used to create a web }

\put(353.83,-519.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}an email and verification code in the request }
\put(353.83,-529.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}body, which are used to verify the user. }
\put(331.87,-546.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- It queries the MySQL database to check if the }
\put(353.83,-557.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}provided email and verification code match }
\put(353.83,-568.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}any records in the Customer\_Info table. }
\put(331.87,-585.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- If a matching record is found, it responds with }
\put(353.83,-596.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a status code 200 and indicates that the }
\put(353.83,-607.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}verification is successful by setting isVerified }
\put(353.83,-618.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}to true. }
\put(331.87,-635.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- If no matching record is found, it responds }
\put(353.83,-646.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}with a status code 400 and an error message }
\put(353.83,-657.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}indicating that the verification code is }
\put(353.83,-668.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}incorrect. }
\put(300.67,-685.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-702.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-719.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-735.936){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\end{picture}

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(277.73,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}27 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-53.40002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3. AI }
\put(44.064,-67.56){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1. Purpose }
\put(44.064,-84.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} Our team has developed an efficient deep learning }
\put(44.064,-95.41998){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model based on the EfficientNet architecture to predict }
\put(44.064,-106.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the stage of hair loss and scalp condition. EfficientNet is }
\put(44.064,-117.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}a model designed with a balance between performance }
\put(44.064,-128.3){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and model size, and the B0 version represents the most }
\put(44.064,-139.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}lightweight variant. This architecture ensures high }
\put(44.064,-150.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}accuracy while efficiently utilizing computational }
\put(44.064,-161.06){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}resources. The model is optimized to learn the features }
\put(44.064,-171.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}necessary for predicting hair loss. }
\put(44.064,-188.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} A convolutional neural network (CNN) is }
\put(44.064,-199.82){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}employed to extract features from images, allowing the }
\put(44.064,-210.74){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model to learn useful patterns and features from input }
\put(44.064,-221.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}images. Specifically, the use of EfficientNetB0 }
\put(44.064,-232.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}facilitates efficient feature extraction, contributing to }
\put(44.064,-243.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}high-efficiency learning by identifying crucial }
\put(44.064,-254.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}information related to hair loss. Adaptive pooling further }
\put(44.064,-265.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enables the model to adapt to various input image sizes, }
\put(44.064,-276.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enhancing its flexibility for deployment in diverse }
\put(44.064,-287.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}environments. }
\put(58.464,-304.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-321.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2. Functionality }
\put(58.464,-337.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The model is designed to classify hair loss levels and }
\put(44.064,-348.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}scalp conditions into four classes, labeled 0, 1, 2, and 3. }
\put(44.064,-359.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Stage 0 represents a normal state, stage 1 indicates mild }
\put(44.064,-370.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}conditions, stage 2 corresponds to moderate conditions, }
\put(44.064,-381.65){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and stage 3 signifies severe conditions. After training the }
\put(44.064,-392.57){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model, it was tested using scalp images of individuals }
\put(44.064,-403.49){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}who have undergone actual hair loss diagnoses. }
\put(58.464,-420.41){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The hyperparameters were further fine-tuned to }
\put(44.064,-431.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}enhance the accuracy of the model. This involved }
\put(44.064,-442.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}adjusting various parameters to achieve better }
\put(44.064,-453.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}performance. The testing phase involved evaluating the }
\put(44.064,-464.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model's performance on scalp images from individuals }
\put(44.064,-475.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}who have received real hair loss diagnoses. }
\put(58.464,-492.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-508.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3. Location of source code }
\put(58.464,-525.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- https://github.com/SEproject-Medihair/Back\_End }
\end{picture}

\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(58.464,-542.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(44.064,-559.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}4. Class component  }
\put(49.224,-577.39){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• API\_Server.py }
\put(49.224,-594.31){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Libraries Used and Their Purpose: }
\put(60.864,-611.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Flask: Flask is a micro web framework for }
\put(82.824,-622.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Python used for building web applications. In }
\put(82.824,-633.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}this code, it's used to create a web API for }
\put(82.824,-644.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}image classification. }
\put(60.864,-660.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- torch: PyTorch is a deep learning framework. }
\put(82.824,-671.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In this code, it's used for loading pre-trained }
\put(82.824,-682.78){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}neural network models and performing }
\put(82.824,-693.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}inference on images. }
\put(60.864,-710.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- transforms (from torchvision): It is used to }
\put(82.824,-721.54){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}define a series of image transformations to }
\put(82.824,-732.456){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}preprocess input images before feeding them }
\put(82.824,-743.376){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}into the neural network. }
\put(331.87,-51.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- PIL (Python Imaging Library): PIL is used for }
\put(353.83,-62.88){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}opening and manipulating images. }
\put(331.87,-79.82001){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- EfficientNet (from efficientnet\_pytorch): This }
\put(353.83,-90.73999){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}library contains the EfficientNet neural }
\put(353.83,-101.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}network architecture, which is used for image }
\put(353.83,-112.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}classification. }
\put(320.23,-129.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Code's Purpose: }
\put(331.87,-146.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- This code creates a Flask web application that }
\put(353.83,-157.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}exposes an endpoint for image classification. }
\put(331.87,-174.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- It defines a function preprocess\_image that }
\put(353.83,-185.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}takes an image file, performs various }
\put(353.83,-196.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}transformations (resize, flip, rotate, etc.), and }
\put(353.83,-207.02){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}converts it into a tensor suitable for neural }
\put(353.83,-217.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}network input. }
\put(331.87,-234.86){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Two functions, predict\_image and }
\put(353.83,-245.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}predict\_image2, are defined to perform image }
\put(353.83,-256.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}classification using pre-trained neural network }
\put(353.83,-267.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}models. These functions take the model and }
\put(353.83,-278.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the preprocessed input tensor, and return the }
\put(353.83,-289.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}predicted class and probabilities of the image }
\put(353.83,-300.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}belonging to different classes. }
\put(331.87,-317.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- Pre-trained EfficientNet models (model and }
\put(353.83,-328.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}model2) for image classification are loaded }
\put(353.83,-339.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}from files (aram\_model6\_architecture.pth and }
\put(353.83,-350.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}aram\_model1\_architecture.pth) using }
\put(353.83,-361.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}PyTorch. }
\put(331.87,-378.05){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}- The /predict route in the Flask app accepts }
\put(353.83,-388.97){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}image files as POST requests, preprocesses }
\put(353.83,-399.89){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}them using preprocess\_image, and performs }
\put(353.83,-410.81){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}classification using the loaded models }
\put(353.83,-421.73){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}(predict\_image and predict\_image2). It then }
\put(353.83,-432.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}returns the predicted classes. }
\put(300.67,-449.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(300.67,-467.23){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• aram\_model1\_architecture.pth }
\put(315.07,-484.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The aram\_model1\_architecture.pth file used in this }
\put(300.67,-496.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}code is a pretrained machine learning model file.  }
\put(315.07,-507.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(315.07,-519.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1) Input and Preprocessing }
\put(337.03,-530.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}This model takes an image file as input. The }
\put(337.03,-542.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}image is preprocessed to prepare it for analysis. }
\put(337.03,-553.63){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The preprocessing steps include resizing the }
\put(337.03,-565.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}image to a specific dimension, applying data }
\put(337.03,-576.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}augmentation techniques like horizontal and }
\put(337.03,-588.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}vertical flips, rotation, and affine transformations, }
\put(337.03,-599.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}converting the image to a tensor, and normalizing }
\put(337.03,-611.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}it. }
\put(315.07,-622.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2) Analysis }
\put(337.03,-634.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The model is designed to analyze the state of the }
\put(337.03,-645.7){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}scalp and hair based on the provided image. It }
\put(337.03,-657.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}performs a detailed analysis and provides an }
\put(337.03,-668.62){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}output prediction. The output is a class label, }
\put(337.03,-680.14){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}which can be one of the following: 0, 1, 2, or 3. }
\put(337.03,-691.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}Each class label corresponds to a different }
\put(337.03,-703.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}assessment or state of the scalp and hair. }
\put(315.07,-714.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3) Training Data }
\put(337.03,-726.1){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}During the development of this AI model, it was }
\put(337.03,-737.616){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}trained on a dataset that included images }
\put(337.03,-749.136){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}representing different stages (0, 1, 2, 3) of scalp }
\end{picture}

\begin{tikzpicture}[overlay]\path(0pt,0pt);\end{tikzpicture}
\begin{picture}(-5,0)(2.5,0)
\put(282.65,-34.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(277.73,-781.416){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}28 }
\put(273.65,-792.96){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(66.024,-52.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and hair conditions. The model learned from these }
\put(66.024,-63.96002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}images to classify new, unseen images into one of }
\put(66.024,-75.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}these stages. }
\put(44.064,-86.90002){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}In summary, aram\_model1\_architecture.pth is a }
\put(29.64,-98.41998){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}pretrained machine learning model used for analyzing scalp }
\put(29.64,-109.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and hair conditions based on input images. It has been }
\put(29.64,-121.46){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}trained on a dataset containing images of different scalp }
\put(29.64,-132.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and hair conditions, allowing it to make predictions about }
\put(29.64,-144.38){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the condition of new images. }
\put(29.64,-155.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(29.64,-167.66){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}• aram\_model6\_architecture.pth }
\put(44.064,-184.58){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The aram\_model6\_architecture.pth file, like the }
\put(29.64,-195.5){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}aram\_model1\_architecture.pth file, is also a pretrained }
\put(29.64,-206.42){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}machine learning model. However, while both models are }
\put(29.64,-217.34){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}used for analyzing scalp and hair conditions, there are key }
\put(29.64,-228.26){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}differences in their specific applications and functionalities: }
\put(44.064,-245.18){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}1. Specific Focus on Hair Loss Stages: The primary }
\put(62.064,-256.13){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}distinction of aram\_model6\_architecture.pth is its }
\put(62.064,-267.17){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}specialization in categorizing stages of hair loss. It }
\put(62.064,-278.09){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}classifies the condition of the scalp and hair into }
\put(62.064,-289.01){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}four distinct stages: 0, 1, 2, and 3. Each stage }
\put(62.064,-299.93){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}represents a different level of hair loss severity. }
\put(44.064,-316.85){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}2. Input and Preprocessing: Similar to aram\_model1\_ }
\put(62.064,-333.77){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}architecture.pth, this model likely takes an image }
\put(62.064,-344.69){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}file as input. The preprocessing steps would be }
\put(62.064,-355.61){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}similar, involving resizing, data augmentation (like }
\put(62.064,-366.53){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}flips, rotation, etc.), converting the image to a tensor, }
\put(62.064,-377.45){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and normalization. }
\put(44.064,-394.37){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}3. Analysis and Output }
\put(62.064,-411.29){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The analysis process of aram\_model6\_ }
\put(62.064,-422.21){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}architecture.pth is focused on identifying the stage }
\put(62.064,-433.15){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of hair loss. It provides an output prediction, }
\put(62.064,-444.07){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}classifying the image into one of the four stages of }
\put(62.064,-454.99){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hair loss. This is the key area where it differs from }
\put(62.064,-465.91){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}aram\_model1\_architecture.pth, which might be }
\put(62.064,-476.83){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}analyzing general scalp and hair conditions without }
\put(62.064,-487.75){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the specific focus on hair loss stages. }
\put(44.064,-504.67){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}4. Training Data }
\put(62.064,-521.59){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}The training data for aram\_model6\_architecture.pth }
\put(62.064,-532.51){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}would consist of images specifically categorized }
\put(62.064,-543.43){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}into the four stages of hair loss. This targeted }
\put(62.064,-554.35){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}dataset allows the model to learn and predict the }
\put(62.064,-565.27){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}hair loss stage of new, unseen images. }
\put(29.64,-582.19){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} In summary, while both aram\_model1\_architecture.pth }
\put(29.64,-593.11){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}and aram\_model6\_architecture.pth are machine learning }
\put(29.64,-604.03){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}models for scalp and hair analysis, aram\_model6\_ }
\put(29.64,-614.98){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}architecture.pth is specifically tailored to classify the stages }
\put(29.64,-625.9){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}of hair loss. This specialized focus is the primary difference }
\put(29.64,-636.94){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}between the two models. }
\put(29.64,-654.22){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791} }
\put(392.59,-52.44){\fontsize{9.96}{1}\usefont{T1}{cmr}{m}{n}\selectfont\color{color_29791}VII. USE CASES }
